# you asked

你是一位尖端的網頁設計師，我現在有一個網頁，使用情形：這個網站的理想目標讀者，應該是「完全沒概念的一般人」，特別是剛好看見這個主題、第一次接觸臉部平權的人。
這不是因為你沒想清楚，而是你在執行一個「倡議引流頁」：目的不是讓已經有背景知識的人來「進階學習」，而是讓那個 「剛好看見這個主題、但平常不會主動搜尋的人」，能在 5–10 分鐘內搞懂：
什麼是臉部平權。
這個議題為什麼和我有關。
我在現實中可以做什麼改變，透過 八張卡片的簡單介紹，來讓點入網站想看看的民眾能知道我們在做 些什麼，但我看到這個網頁，總覺得好像不夠完善，不夠清楚，不 過智能，請你幫我想想看，以一個專業工程師的角度，和我說哪裡 做的不好，該刪除，該更正，該加入，和該加上一些什麼。我這裡的網址和用手機開啟的圖片會一併給你，請燒等我片刻

---

# perplexity response

可以，等你把「網址」和「手機截圖」貼上來，我會直接用「面向完全新手的一頁式倡議引流頁」這個標準幫你做完整檢查。

我會重點幫你看這幾件事：新手能不能在 5–10 分鐘內看懂「什麼是臉部平權」、網站有沒有清楚回答「這跟我有什麼關係」、八張卡片的資訊架構是否太散或太重、手機版的閱讀節奏是否順、CTA 是否夠明確，以及哪些內容該刪、該改寫、該補上。

你貼過來後，我會直接給你這種格式的回饋：
- 哪裡做得不好
- 哪些內容應該刪掉
- 哪些文案應該改寫
- 應該新增哪些區塊
- 八張卡片要怎麼重排
- 手機版 UI/UX 哪裡卡住
- 如果要，我也可以進一步幫你產出「改版線框」或「直接重寫成更好的頁面文案」

請直接貼：
- 網址
- 手機截圖（可多張）
- 如果有的話，也一起貼目前你最不滿意的地方，這樣我會抓得更準。

# you asked

先看看這些，我再繼續上傳

---

# perplexity response

如果你的目標真的是「讓剛好滑到的人在 5–10 分鐘內懂這件事」，那現在這個版本比較像是**已經對議題有點興趣的人，願意慢慢逛的專題頁**，而不是一個對陌生訪客高效轉譯的倡議引流頁。[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=WIXo9qmTaBOcg%2B4zrKqUmCFRDNM%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWac ## 先說優點

你現在的網站有幾個地方其實做得不錯：整體色彩辨識度高，黑底配黃橘色讓議題感與活動感很明確；卡片化也有把內容切塊，對手機閱讀比長段文字友善；另外你已經有把內容分成「認識概念、情境案例、要／不要、延伸參考」等層次，代表你不是亂堆資訊，而是有在想教學順序。[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=WIXo9qmTaBOcg%2B4zrKqUmCFRDNM%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F% 首屏主標「不要看一張臉，要看一個人」也很有記憶點，這句話有倡議標語的力量，能留下印象。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=VFHNmY84pLMhAWLzehA9%2BnxP5JU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFt ## 最大問題

### 首屏沒有先解決新手的三個問題

第一次進來的人，腦中通常只有三件事：「這是什麼？為什麼跟我有關？我現在要看哪裡？」但你目前首屏雖然有大標語和 CTA，**卻沒有用最短時間把這三件事說透**。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

「什麼是臉部平權？」有出現在標題，但下面的說明句偏長，而且概念密度高；對完全陌生的人來說，還是要多花一點力氣解碼。 「不要看一張臉，要看一個人」很有力量，但它偏倡議口號，不等於定義，所以首屏會出現「有感覺，但還沒完全懂」的狀態。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

### 資訊很多，但導航線不夠單純

從你給的截圖看，頁面裡有「我們在做什麼」、「8 個問題快速了解」、「真實情境」、「要／不要」、「延伸參考」等模組，內容本身不算少。 問題是對新手來說，這些模組之間目前比較像「都很重要」，而不是「先看 A，再懂 B，最後去做 C」。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2e5c063d-9e6d-411d-9329-b707d2073194/1000009351.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=NKbhiqlnjks17oSDTpdPmZR7%2B3M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FE ### 八張卡片方向對，但卡片文案還不夠「一眼懂」

八張卡片是個很好的形式，因為它很適合新手分段吸收。 但從目前可見的卡片來看，標題有些偏抽象，例如「外貌歧視有哪些常見誤解？」、「這頁面能幫你做什麼？」這種句子是清楚的，但不是最有拉力的說法；它比較像章節名稱，不像一般人會立刻想點的問題。[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2e5c063d-9e6d-411d-9329-b707d2073194/1000009351.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=NKbhiqlnjks17oSDTpdPmZR7%2B3M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVz ## 該刪的

### 刪掉過早出現的次要入口

頁面一開始就出現「先看八大重點」這種按鈕是合理的，但如果同一層還有太多其他選項，會稀釋主路徑。 對新手頁來說，首屏最好只有一條最明顯的入口，例如「3 分鐘先搞懂」或「先看 8 個重點」，而不是讓使用者自己判斷哪個比較適合。[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=dne4XHPrftw%2B02orMLhh41ghg9o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiB ### 刪掉不必要的抽象修飾句

像「用自然、尊重的態度相處，其實比想像中容易」這類句子語氣不差，但如果它出現在太前面，會有點像結論先行，卻沒有先把問題具體化。 對完全陌生的人，前段更需要的是「具體、白話、生活化」，不是先安撫。[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/f5d3f41c-a3a5-4128-ae40-07c2aa5a463f/1000009357.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=FnwS5eBV%2FeOruyO6xoQpkB5WDhk%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=dne4XHPrftw%2B02orMLhh41ghg9o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F ### 刪減重複概念

從截圖看，「認識概念」、「我們在做什麼」、「8 個問題」、「第一次接觸到這類情況可以怎麼互動」之間有一些內容功能其實接近，都在做新手導覽。 這些區塊如果都保留，但各自都講一點定義、講一點教學，會讓整體節奏變散。[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2e5c063d-9e6d-411d-9329-b707d2073194/1000009351.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=NKbhiqlnjks17oSDTpdPmZR7%2B3M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=1mLQR77ybqpdGzCIPW4VuQpDedI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F ## 該更正的

### Hero 文案要更像「新手翻譯」

你現在的首屏標語適合保留，但它下面應該補一段**超白話副標**，直接把概念翻成一般人的日常語言。 例如方向應該是：「臉部平權，就是不要因為一個人的長相、臉部特徵或外貌差異，就先入為主地貼標籤、排斥或不公平對待。」這種句子比目前更像第一層解釋。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

### 「要／不要」區塊要再更生活化

這區其實很有潛力，因為它直接回答「我在現實中可以做什麼改變」。 但現在看起來比較像原則整理，還可以再往「我真的會遇到的場景」推近一點，例如朋友聚會、職場面試、陌生人注視、孩子提問等。[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=VFHNmY84pLMhAWLzehA9%2BnxP5JU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F% ### Menu 文案需要站在首次訪客角度命名

側邊選單現在有「臉部平權」、「職場臉部平權指引」、「陽光基金會官網」等項目。 對熟人來說沒問題，但對新手來說，第一項如果只是「臉部平權」，資訊含量太少；更好的是把它改成「3 分鐘認識臉部平權」或「先了解：臉部平權是什麼」。[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/53c0471b-8ebf-4c77-9841-6352991561d9/1000009341.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ZpEinVk24oibAJZmpPHtq861It0%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 該加入的

### 加一個「你為什麼要在意」區塊

這是目前我覺得最應該補的東西之一。雖然你有談概念和情境，但還沒有很明確地用一個短區塊回答：「這不只是少數人的議題，而是每個人都可能在日常中參與、旁觀或改變的事。」[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGM 這區可以用 3 個最短句：
- 你可能無意間說過讓人受傷的話。
- 你可能看過別人被盯著看、被取笑，卻不知道怎麼幫忙。
- 你也可以用更好的互動方式，讓對方少受一次傷。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=VFHNmY84pLMhAWLzehA9%2BnxP5JU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7 ### 加一條超清楚的閱讀路線

你既然希望民眾在 5–10 分鐘內看懂，就應該明講閱讀路徑，例如：「第一次來，建議這樣看：先懂概念 → 看真實情境 → 學會怎麼互動 → 需要時再延伸閱讀。」這會大幅降低陌生訪客的認知負擔。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=1mLQR77ybqpdGzCIPW4VuQpDedI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/f5d3f41c-a3a5-4128-ae40-07c2aa5a463f/1000009357.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=FnwS5eBV%2FeOruyO6xoQpkB5WDhk%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAi ### 加「一分鐘版本」摘要

不是每個人都會真的滑完整頁。 所以很建議在前 2 個畫面內放一個「一分鐘先懂」的小模組，用 3–4 個 bullet 就講完核心：是什麼、為什麼重要、我能做什麼。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=1mLQR77ybqpdGzCIPW4VuQpDedI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7 ## 八張卡片怎麼改

可以改成這個順序：
1. 什麼是臉部平權？
2. 為什麼這不只是「外貌」問題？
3. 這件事在台灣常見嗎？
4. 當事人會遇到什麼情況？
5. 為什麼有些話其實會傷人？
6. 第一次遇到時可以怎麼互動？
7. 日常生活裡我可以怎麼做？
8. ## 手機版 UI 問題

### 首屏資訊密度偏高

Hero 區有導覽條、活動標籤、主標、說明、兩個按鈕，手機上第一眼稍微擠。 視覺上是有層次的，但對陌生讀者來說，要先理解哪個最重要，還要花半秒判斷。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

### 文字對比與字級還能再優化

卡片內灰字在黑底上有些偏淡，對年齡層稍廣的一般讀者不夠友善。 而且有些段落在手機寬度下行長略長，導致閱讀節奏會拖。[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=dne4XHPrftw%2B02orMLhh41ghg9o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=WIXo9qmTaBOcg%2B4zrKqUmCFRDNM%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5cs ### 橫向滑動需要更強提示

「這些情境，真的會發生」那區有提示「左右滑動查看更多」，這是對的，但目前卡片截斷呈現方式容易讓人知道「好像可以滑」，卻不一定很想滑。 這種區塊通常要再強化一點可滑動的視覺暗示，或改成更適合手機連續閱讀的直向堆疊。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 我最建議你下一版先改的 5 件事

- 重寫首屏副標，用最白話的方式定義「臉部平權」。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)
- 分鐘內懂這件事」，那現在這個版本比較像是**已經對議題有點興趣的人，願意慢慢逛的專題頁**，而不是一個對陌生訪客高效轉譯的倡議引流頁。[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=WIXo9qmTaBOcg%2B4zrKqUmCFRDNM%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWac ## 先說優點

你現在的網站有幾個地方其實做得不錯：整體色彩辨識度高，黑底配黃橘色讓議題感與活動感很明確；卡片化也有把內容切塊，對手機閱讀比長段文字友善；另外你已經有把內容分成「認識概念、情境案例、要／不要、延伸參考」等層次，代表你不是亂堆資訊，而是有在想教學順序。[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=WIXo9qmTaBOcg%2B4zrKqUmCFRDNM%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F% 首屏主標「不要看一張臉，要看一個人」也很有記憶點，這句話有倡議標語的力量，能留下印象。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=VFHNmY84pLMhAWLzehA9%2BnxP5JU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFt ## 最大問題

### 首屏沒有先解決新手的三個問題

第一次進來的人，腦中通常只有三件事：「這是什麼？為什麼跟我有關？我現在要看哪裡？」但你目前首屏雖然有大標語和 CTA，**卻沒有用最短時間把這三件事說透**。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

「什麼是臉部平權？」有出現在標題，但下面的說明句偏長，而且概念密度高；對完全陌生的人來說，還是要多花一點力氣解碼。 「不要看一張臉，要看一個人」很有力量，但它偏倡議口號，不等於定義，所以首屏會出現「有感覺，但還沒完全懂」的狀態。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

### 資訊很多，但導航線不夠單純

從你給的截圖看，頁面裡有「我們在做什麼」、「8 個問題快速了解」、「真實情境」、「要／不要」、「延伸參考」等模組，內容本身不算少。 問題是對新手來說，這些模組之間目前比較像「都很重要」，而不是「先看 A，再懂 B，最後去做 C」。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2e5c063d-9e6d-411d-9329-b707d2073194/1000009351.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=NKbhiqlnjks17oSDTpdPmZR7%2B3M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FE ### 八張卡片方向對，但卡片文案還不夠「一眼懂」

八張卡片是個很好的形式，因為它很適合新手分段吸收。 但從目前可見的卡片來看，標題有些偏抽象，例如「外貌歧視有哪些常見誤解？」、「這頁面能幫你做什麼？」這種句子是清楚的，但不是最有拉力的說法；它比較像章節名稱，不像一般人會立刻想點的問題。[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2e5c063d-9e6d-411d-9329-b707d2073194/1000009351.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=NKbhiqlnjks17oSDTpdPmZR7%2B3M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVz ## 該刪的

### 刪掉過早出現的次要入口

頁面一開始就出現「先看八大重點」這種按鈕是合理的，但如果同一層還有太多其他選項，會稀釋主路徑。 對新手頁來說，首屏最好只有一條最明顯的入口，例如「3 分鐘先搞懂」或「先看 8 個重點」，而不是讓使用者自己判斷哪個比較適合。[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=dne4XHPrftw%2B02orMLhh41ghg9o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiB ### 刪掉不必要的抽象修飾句

像「用自然、尊重的態度相處，其實比想像中容易」這類句子語氣不差，但如果它出現在太前面，會有點像結論先行，卻沒有先把問題具體化。 對完全陌生的人，前段更需要的是「具體、白話、生活化」，不是先安撫。[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/f5d3f41c-a3a5-4128-ae40-07c2aa5a463f/1000009357.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=FnwS5eBV%2FeOruyO6xoQpkB5WDhk%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=dne4XHPrftw%2B02orMLhh41ghg9o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F ### 刪減重複概念

從截圖看，「認識概念」、「我們在做什麼」、「8 個問題」、「第一次接觸到這類情況可以怎麼互動」之間有一些內容功能其實接近，都在做新手導覽。 這些區塊如果都保留，但各自都講一點定義、講一點教學，會讓整體節奏變散。[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2e5c063d-9e6d-411d-9329-b707d2073194/1000009351.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=NKbhiqlnjks17oSDTpdPmZR7%2B3M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=1mLQR77ybqpdGzCIPW4VuQpDedI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F ## 該更正的

### Hero 文案要更像「新手翻譯」

你現在的首屏標語適合保留，但它下面應該補一段**超白話副標**，直接把概念翻成一般人的日常語言。 例如方向應該是：「臉部平權，就是不要因為一個人的長相、臉部特徵或外貌差異，就先入為主地貼標籤、排斥或不公平對待。」這種句子比目前更像第一層解釋。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

### 「要／不要」區塊要再更生活化

這區其實很有潛力，因為它直接回答「我在現實中可以做什麼改變」。 但現在看起來比較像原則整理，還可以再往「我真的會遇到的場景」推近一點，例如朋友聚會、職場面試、陌生人注視、孩子提問等。[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=VFHNmY84pLMhAWLzehA9%2BnxP5JU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F% ### Menu 文案需要站在首次訪客角度命名

側邊選單現在有「臉部平權」、「職場臉部平權指引」、「陽光基金會官網」等項目。 對熟人來說沒問題，但對新手來說，第一項如果只是「臉部平權」，資訊含量太少；更好的是把它改成「3 分鐘認識臉部平權」或「先了解：臉部平權是什麼」。[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/53c0471b-8ebf-4c77-9841-6352991561d9/1000009341.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ZpEinVk24oibAJZmpPHtq861It0%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 該加入的

### 加一個「你為什麼要在意」區塊

這是目前我覺得最應該補的東西之一。雖然你有談概念和情境，但還沒有很明確地用一個短區塊回答：「這不只是少數人的議題，而是每個人都可能在日常中參與、旁觀或改變的事。」[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=TU%2BEoHNZN3uFRTNEnC8md24HJMw%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGM 這區可以用 3 個最短句：
- 你可能無意間說過讓人受傷的話。
- 你可能看過別人被盯著看、被取笑，卻不知道怎麼幫忙。
- 你也可以用更好的互動方式，讓對方少受一次傷。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=VFHNmY84pLMhAWLzehA9%2BnxP5JU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7 ### 加一條超清楚的閱讀路線

你既然希望民眾在 5–10 分鐘內看懂，就應該明講閱讀路徑，例如：「第一次來，建議這樣看：先懂概念 → 看真實情境 → 學會怎麼互動 → 需要時再延伸閱讀。」這會大幅降低陌生訪客的認知負擔。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=1mLQR77ybqpdGzCIPW4VuQpDedI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/f5d3f41c-a3a5-4128-ae40-07c2aa5a463f/1000009357.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=FnwS5eBV%2FeOruyO6xoQpkB5WDhk%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAi ### 加「一分鐘版本」摘要

不是每個人都會真的滑完整頁。 所以很建議在前 2 個畫面內放一個「一分鐘先懂」的小模組，用 3–4 個 bullet 就講完核心：是什麼、為什麼重要、我能做什麼。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=1mLQR77ybqpdGzCIPW4VuQpDedI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7 ## 八張卡片怎麼改

可以改成這個順序：
1. 什麼是臉部平權？
2. 為什麼這不只是「外貌」問題？
3. 這件事在台灣常見嗎？
4. 當事人會遇到什麼情況？
5. 為什麼有些話其實會傷人？
6. 第一次遇到時可以怎麼互動？
7. 日常生活裡我可以怎麼做？
8. ## 手機版 UI 問題

### 首屏資訊密度偏高

Hero 區有導覽條、活動標籤、主標、說明、兩個按鈕，手機上第一眼稍微擠。 視覺上是有層次的，但對陌生讀者來說，要先理解哪個最重要，還要花半秒判斷。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

### 文字對比與字級還能再優化

卡片內灰字在黑底上有些偏淡，對年齡層稍廣的一般讀者不夠友善。 而且有些段落在手機寬度下行長略長，導致閱讀節奏會拖。[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=dne4XHPrftw%2B02orMLhh41ghg9o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=WIXo9qmTaBOcg%2B4zrKqUmCFRDNM%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5cs
