### 橫向滑動需要更強提示

「這些情境，真的會發生」那區有提示「左右滑動查看更多」，這是對的，但目前卡片截斷呈現方式容易讓人知道「好像可以滑」，卻不一定很想滑。 這種區塊通常要再強化一點可滑動的視覺暗示，或改成更適合手機連續閱讀的直向堆疊。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=DiUXtP4ANCqUimBwpUiAUy4sWBU%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 我最建議你下一版先改的 5 件事

- 重寫首屏副標，用最白話的方式定義「臉部平權」。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=JV5nXMdSc9vWEJVXejWBm%2BWum5o%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)
- # you asked

https://jovial-sprite-41d8ad.netlify.app/

# perplexity response

我看完你補的截圖和網站首頁後，判斷更明確了：**這個網站現在已經比一般學生作品完整很多，但它還沒有完全做到「倡議引流頁」最重要的事——用最短時間把陌生人成功帶進來。** 如果你要的是「讓平常不會主動搜尋的人，也願意花 5–10 分鐘看懂，甚至願意往下做一點事」，那我會說：**你的問題不是內容不夠，而是內容太平均；每一段都像重點，反而沒有真正的主重點。**[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4b25b15e-20ee-43ea-aec9-0fd99f0d59f6/1000009369.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=SSYBvSgr9hfAvXzY0YPOl0c2zL0%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jq ## 整體判斷

這個頁面其實已經具備不少正確元素：有明確主題、有八張卡片導覽、有三不三要、有真實案例、有數據、有影片、有延伸資源，內容面很完整。 但對第一次接觸的人來說，完整不等於好吸收，尤其手機上更容易出現「資訊都很重要，所以我不知道先看哪裡」的狀況。[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3 你現在的頁面比較像一個「把所有該講的都講到」的網站；而倡議引流頁更像一個「先讓陌生人願意留下來，再讓他一步一步理解」的網站。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa% ## 你做得好的地方

### 議題定位清楚

首頁標題已經直接定義臉部平權是「不因外貌而差別對待」，這點比很多倡議網站清楚，也比只喊口號更有效。 「每張臉都該被公平對待」這句也有記憶點，適合當價值主張。

### 有把抽象議題拆成入口

「三件事讓你五秒看懂」、「八個問題快速理解」、「第一次接觸可以怎麼互動」這些設計，代表你有意識地把內容拆成新手可進入的區塊，這方向是對的。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)

### 真實案例與數據都有放進來

求職被拒、異樣眼光、復健歷程、民調數字、陽光基金會歷史與服務量，這些都能幫議題從抽象價值變成現實問題。 這是很重要的，因為倡議如果只有理念沒有證據，說服力會弱很多。[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/b1c9a821-55b3-4488-9926-f9dde4a9d528/1000009361.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=5x1Ky6026WFp41n5xLVml%2FtCXM8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5 5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 真正不夠好的地方

### 首屏還是不夠像「新手頁」

雖然首頁已經有定義，但首屏同時放了活動標籤、主標、描述、按鈕、上方導覽列，資訊層級還是偏多。 對第一次進來的人來說，第一眼最需要的是一句極白話定義、一句「這和你有關」、一個超明確下一步；你現在有做到第一項的一半，但第二、三項還不夠狠。[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)

更直接地說：**我知道你在講一個重要議題，但我還沒有被快速說服「我現在就該看下去」。**[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)

### 「三件事」區塊功能重複

「三件事讓你五秒看懂這個網站」和後面的「八個問題快速理解臉部平權」在功能上有點重疊，兩者都在扮演導覽。 前者偏網站介紹，後者偏議題導覽，但對一般人來說差異沒有大到需要分成兩套入口。[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)

結果就是你前面還在熱身，使用者卻已經開始覺得內容很多。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)

### 八張卡片仍然偏「編輯視角」

八張卡片的分類本身不錯，但還是比較像策展者在分主題，不像一般人腦中的問題順序。 例如「背景」、「資源」、「故事」是網站編排合理的分類，但陌生人比較會想的是：「這到底是什麼？常見嗎？我是不是也做過？遇到時怎麼辦？」

也就是說，你的卡片是清楚的，但還不夠貼近新手的心理流程。[[11]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)

### 內容密度高，但掃讀支援不足

你有很多段落其實內容很好，可是在手機上看會顯得偏重，尤其卡片說明、案例內文、資源列表區塊都需要逐字讀。 對倡議引流頁來說，應該更大量利用「一句話結論＋必要時再展開」的寫法，而不是讓每個區塊一開始就承擔太多閱讀負擔。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/60504cda-44e8-4601-a638-dacabb88d351/1000009373.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=lTTs4Xl%2Bwv2FadhJDjVfA1cpUWY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2B ### 末段資源太像資料庫，不像行動收束

「依需求，深入認識臉部平權」這區很完整，還區分官方資源、深入閱讀、立即參與、給特定角色。 但它現在比較像一份整理得不錯的清單，缺少一個更強的收束句：**看完之後，你最推薦一般人做的第一件事是什麼？**[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/ef86598b-03bd-4ca6-94c3-0e660a5e3da0/1000009375.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=Eah%2FRCNlwFSH%2F%2F7Wp1dbly7t2HI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2 倡議頁最後不能只是「這裡有很多連結」，而要是「如果你只做一件事，請先做這件事」。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQT ## 該刪除的

### 刪掉前段的雙重導覽

我會建議二選一：保留「三件事讓你五秒看懂」或保留「八個問題快速理解」，不要兩個都那麼前面。 如果目標是新手，我傾向保留「八個問題」作為主體，把「三件事」縮成非常短的三個 bullet，直接併進 Hero 下方。[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)

### 刪減過多的次要按鈕與分流

像「更多相關影片」、「前往 YouTube 頻道」、「更多互動建議」、「了解職場平權」、「閱讀起源」這類連結都不是不能有，但不要太早大量出現，不然主線會被打散。 新手在還沒建立完整認知前，被太多外部延伸點吸走，其實很容易中途離開。[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6yc ### 刪掉部分重複性的說明句

有些文案是在講同一件事，例如「先看見人，再看見外表」、「不因外貌差別對待」、「每張臉都該被公平對待」，概念一致是好事，但頁面上重複太多次會稀釋新鮮度。 建議保留一句最強的當主標語，其他地方改講更具體的內容。

## 該更正的

### Hero 應該補上「這跟你有關」

現在 Hero 講清楚了議題，但還少一句把讀者拉進來的話。 我會建議在主標下方直接補一句像這樣的副標方向：**「你不一定認識顏損者，但你一定遇過以貌取人的文化；臉部平權，就是從日常互動開始改變。」** 這句的功能是把旁觀者變成利害關係人。[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)

### 卡片標題要更口語

例如「為什麼台灣需要臉部平權運動？」可以改成「這件事真的常發生嗎？」；「你能從日常生活做什麼改變？」可以改成「如果我是一般人，我能做什麼？」；「外貌歧視有哪些常見誤解？」可以改成「有些你以為沒惡意的反應，其實會傷人嗎？」 這樣點擊意願會更高，因為更像使用者心裡真的會冒出的問題。

### 數據區應該更「翻譯化」

現在數據本身很有力，像 1/5、9,000+、45 年都很好。 但它的呈現還可以更貼近一般人，例如不是只寫「每 5 人中，就有 1 人…」，而是直接翻譯成「這不是少數人才會遇到的事」。[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4b25b15e-20ee-43ea-aec9-0fd99f0d59f6/1000009369.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=SSYBvSgr9hfAvXzY0YPOl0c2zL0%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/b1c9a821-55b3-4488-9926-f9dde4a9d528/1000009361.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=5x1Ky6026WFp41n5xLVml%2FtCXM8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAi ## 該加入的

### 加一個「你可能也遇過」區塊

這會非常有用。你可以列 4 個超短情境，讓一般人瞬間意識到這件事不遙遠：
- 面試時先看外表再判斷專業。
- 看到疤痕就一直盯著看。
- 用「你以前怎麼了」當開場白。
- 把外貌差異當成玩笑話題。[[12]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg)[[13]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg)[[14]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg)[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

這種區塊的功能不是教育知識，而是建立「原來我也在這個文化裡」的自我連結。

### 加「只看 1 分鐘版」

如果有人不想完整看八張卡片，你應該給他一個極短版本。 例如：
- 臉部平權：不因外貌差異而差別對待。
- 它很常見：每 5 人就有 1 人曾因外貌受不友善對待。
- 它和你有關：你每天的眼神、問題、玩笑、選擇都會影響別人。
- 你可以做的：不盯視、不追問、自然互動、尊重對待。

### 加最後的單一 CTA

目前末段有很多資源，但沒有一個壓倒性的「下一步」。 你應該選一個最符合頁面目標的 CTA，例如「先讀三不三要」、「簽署支持」、「分享給一個朋友」，而不是同時把所有參與方式放成差不多重。[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/60504cda-44e8-4601-a638-dacabb88d351/1000009373.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=lTTs4Xl%2Bwv2FadhJDjVfA1cpUWY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U ## 八張卡片重排建議

如果你的受眾是完全沒概念的人，我會建議八張卡片改成下面這個順序，讓理解更順：

| 現在要達成的心理任務 | 建議卡片標題 |
|---|---|
| 先懂定義 | 什麼是臉部平權？ |
| 建立關聯 | 這件事為什麼和我有關？ |
| 打破誤解 | 有些你以為沒惡意的反應，為什麼會傷人？ |
| 看到普遍性 | 這件事在台灣常見嗎？ |
| 看見現實 | 顏損者日常真的會遇到什麼？ |
| 學會互動 | 第一次接觸時，我可以怎麼做？ |
| 轉成行動 | 在學校、職場、社群裡我能做什麼？ |
| 再往下走 | 如果你想更深入，從這裡開始 |

這種排法的關鍵是：每張卡片都在解決一個「下一步問題」，不是只在分類內容。

## 手機 UI/UX 建議

### 導覽列太搶首屏注意力

上方導覽列的存在感很強，尤其黃色按鈕與深色底反差很高，會先搶走一部分焦點。 這對功能導向網站可以接受，但對倡議頁來說，Hero 主張應該是最先被記住的。[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E0 ### 卡片陰影、描邊與內文對比可再精簡

現在卡片很多都用了深色底、淡描邊、亮色標題、灰色內文。 問題不是醜，而是當整頁很多區塊都長得有點像時，閱讀節奏會變得平。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[11]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg)[[12]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/a ### 橫滑卡片不適合承載太重要資訊

「真實的聲音」區塊有價值，但如果這些案例是很重要的說服材料，放在橫向滑動裡會降低實際被看完的機率。 手機用戶不是不會滑，而是很多人看見可滑區塊只會滑 1 次就結束。[[13]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg)[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 我會怎麼改版

如果我是你這頁的設計／前端顧問，我會先做這個優先順序：

- 第一優先：重寫首屏與 Hero 下方的「一分鐘理解區」。[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)
- 第二優先：把「三件事」與「八張卡片」整併成一條更明確的新手主線。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)
- 第三優先：把真實案例改成更容易讀完的呈現，別太依賴橫滑。[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[13]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg)

## 你下一步最值得做的事

我建議你現在不要先急著修視覺細節，先做**資訊架構重整**。 因為你目前最大的瓶頸不是樣式，而是「陌生人閱讀時被帶去哪裡」這件事還不夠精準。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)

如果你要，我下一則可以直接幫你做下面其中一種：
- 直接列出「首頁每一區：保留／刪除／改寫／新增」清單。
- 幫你重寫整個首頁文案架構。
- 幫你重排八張卡片，連每張標題和 2 句說明都寫好。
- 用「專業 UI/UX review」格式，逐段評論這個網址的資訊架構、文案、互動與手機版問題。

如果你要最實用的，我建議下一步我直接幫你做：**「保留／刪除／改寫／新增」完整改版表。**

我看完你補的截圖和網站首頁後，判斷更明確了：**這個網站現在已經比一般學生作品完整很多，但它還沒有完全做到「倡議引流頁」最重要的事——用最短時間把陌生人成功帶進來。** 如果你要的是「讓平常不會主動搜尋的人，也願意花 5–10 分鐘看懂，甚至願意往下做一點事」，那我會說：**你的問題不是內容不夠，而是內容太平均；每一段都像重點，反而沒有真正的主重點。**[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4b25b15e-20ee-43ea-aec9-0fd99f0d59f6/1000009369.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=SSYBvSgr9hfAvXzY0YPOl0c2zL0%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jq ## 整體判斷

這個頁面其實已經具備不少正確元素：有明確主題、有八張卡片導覽、有三不三要、有真實案例、有數據、有影片、有延伸資源，內容面很完整。 但對第一次接觸的人來說，完整不等於好吸收，尤其手機上更容易出現「資訊都很重要，所以我不知道先看哪裡」的狀況。[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3 你現在的頁面比較像一個「把所有該講的都講到」的網站；而倡議引流頁更像一個「先讓陌生人願意留下來，再讓他一步一步理解」的網站。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa% ## 你做得好的地方

### 議題定位清楚

首頁標題已經直接定義臉部平權是「不因外貌而差別對待」，這點比很多倡議網站清楚，也比只喊口號更有效。 「每張臉都該被公平對待」這句也有記憶點，適合當價值主張。

### 有把抽象議題拆成入口

「三件事讓你五秒看懂」、「八個問題快速理解」、「第一次接觸可以怎麼互動」這些設計，代表你有意識地把內容拆成新手可進入的區塊，這方向是對的。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)

### 真實案例與數據都有放進來

求職被拒、異樣眼光、復健歷程、民調數字、陽光基金會歷史與服務量，這些都能幫議題從抽象價值變成現實問題。 這是很重要的，因為倡議如果只有理念沒有證據，說服力會弱很多。[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/b1c9a821-55b3-4488-9926-f9dde4a9d528/1000009361.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=5x1Ky6026WFp41n5xLVml%2FtCXM8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5 5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 真正不夠好的地方

### 首屏還是不夠像「新手頁」

雖然首頁已經有定義，但首屏同時放了活動標籤、主標、描述、按鈕、上方導覽列，資訊層級還是偏多。 對第一次進來的人來說，第一眼最需要的是一句極白話定義、一句「這和你有關」、一個超明確下一步；你現在有做到第一項的一半，但第二、三項還不夠狠。[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)

更直接地說：**我知道你在講一個重要議題，但我還沒有被快速說服「我現在就該看下去」。**[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)

### 「三件事」區塊功能重複

「三件事讓你五秒看懂這個網站」和後面的「八個問題快速理解臉部平權」在功能上有點重疊，兩者都在扮演導覽。 前者偏網站介紹，後者偏議題導覽，但對一般人來說差異沒有大到需要分成兩套入口。[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)

結果就是你前面還在熱身，使用者卻已經開始覺得內容很多。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)

### 八張卡片仍然偏「編輯視角」

八張卡片的分類本身不錯，但還是比較像策展者在分主題，不像一般人腦中的問題順序。 例如「背景」、「資源」、「故事」是網站編排合理的分類，但陌生人比較會想的是：「這到底是什麼？常見嗎？我是不是也做過？遇到時怎麼辦？」

也就是說，你的卡片是清楚的，但還不夠貼近新手的心理流程。[[11]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)

### 內容密度高，但掃讀支援不足

你有很多段落其實內容很好，可是在手機上看會顯得偏重，尤其卡片說明、案例內文、資源列表區塊都需要逐字讀。 對倡議引流頁來說，應該更大量利用「一句話結論＋必要時再展開」的寫法，而不是讓每個區塊一開始就承擔太多閱讀負擔。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/60504cda-44e8-4601-a638-dacabb88d351/1000009373.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=lTTs4Xl%2Bwv2FadhJDjVfA1cpUWY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2B ### 末段資源太像資料庫，不像行動收束

「依需求，深入認識臉部平權」這區很完整，還區分官方資源、深入閱讀、立即參與、給特定角色。 但它現在比較像一份整理得不錯的清單，缺少一個更強的收束句：**看完之後，你最推薦一般人做的第一件事是什麼？**[[0]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/ef86598b-03bd-4ca6-94c3-0e660a5e3da0/1000009375.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=Eah%2FRCNlwFSH%2F%2F7Wp1dbly7t2HI%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2 倡議頁最後不能只是「這裡有很多連結」，而要是「如果你只做一件事，請先做這件事」。[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQT ## 該刪除的

### 刪掉前段的雙重導覽

我會建議二選一：保留「三件事讓你五秒看懂」或保留「八個問題快速理解」，不要兩個都那麼前面。 如果目標是新手，我傾向保留「八個問題」作為主體，把「三件事」縮成非常短的三個 bullet，直接併進 Hero 下方。[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)

### 刪減過多的次要按鈕與分流

像「更多相關影片」、「前往 YouTube 頻道」、「更多互動建議」、「了解職場平權」、「閱讀起源」這類連結都不是不能有，但不要太早大量出現，不然主線會被打散。 新手在還沒建立完整認知前，被太多外部延伸點吸走，其實很容易中途離開。[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6yc ### 刪掉部分重複性的說明句

有些文案是在講同一件事，例如「先看見人，再看見外表」、「不因外貌差別對待」、「每張臉都該被公平對待」，概念一致是好事，但頁面上重複太多次會稀釋新鮮度。 建議保留一句最強的當主標語，其他地方改講更具體的內容。

## 該更正的

### Hero 應該補上「這跟你有關」

現在 Hero 講清楚了議題，但還少一句把讀者拉進來的話。 我會建議在主標下方直接補一句像這樣的副標方向：**「你不一定認識顏損者，但你一定遇過以貌取人的文化；臉部平權，就是從日常互動開始改變。」** 這句的功能是把旁觀者變成利害關係人。[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)

### 卡片標題要更口語

例如「為什麼台灣需要臉部平權運動？」可以改成「這件事真的常發生嗎？」；「你能從日常生活做什麼改變？」可以改成「如果我是一般人，我能做什麼？」；「外貌歧視有哪些常見誤解？」可以改成「有些你以為沒惡意的反應，其實會傷人嗎？」 這樣點擊意願會更高，因為更像使用者心裡真的會冒出的問題。

### 數據區應該更「翻譯化」

現在數據本身很有力，像 1/5、9,000+、45 年都很好。 但它的呈現還可以更貼近一般人，例如不是只寫「每 5 人中，就有 1 人…」，而是直接翻譯成「這不是少數人才會遇到的事」。[[2]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4b25b15e-20ee-43ea-aec9-0fd99f0d59f6/1000009369.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=SSYBvSgr9hfAvXzY0YPOl0c2zL0%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[6]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/b1c9a821-55b3-4488-9926-f9dde4a9d528/1000009361.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=5x1Ky6026WFp41n5xLVml%2FtCXM8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAi ## 該加入的

### 加一個「你可能也遇過」區塊

這會非常有用。你可以列 4 個超短情境，讓一般人瞬間意識到這件事不遙遠：
- 面試時先看外表再判斷專業。
- 看到疤痕就一直盯著看。
- 用「你以前怎麼了」當開場白。
- 把外貌差異當成玩笑話題。[[12]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg)[[13]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg)[[14]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/930f7cf9-45d6-432d-ab1c-1012930ae31c/1000009353.jpg)[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

這種區塊的功能不是教育知識，而是建立「原來我也在這個文化裡」的自我連結。

### 加「只看 1 分鐘版」

如果有人不想完整看八張卡片，你應該給他一個極短版本。 例如：
- 臉部平權：不因外貌差異而差別對待。
- 它很常見：每 5 人就有 1 人曾因外貌受不友善對待。
- 它和你有關：你每天的眼神、問題、玩笑、選擇都會影響別人。
- 你可以做的：不盯視、不追問、自然互動、尊重對待。

### 加最後的單一 CTA

目前末段有很多資源，但沒有一個壓倒性的「下一步」。 你應該選一個最符合頁面目標的 CTA，例如「先讀三不三要」、「簽署支持」、「分享給一個朋友」，而不是同時把所有參與方式放成差不多重。[[5]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/60504cda-44e8-4601-a638-dacabb88d351/1000009373.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=lTTs4Xl%2Bwv2FadhJDjVfA1cpUWY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U ## 八張卡片重排建議

如果你的受眾是完全沒概念的人，我會建議八張卡片改成下面這個順序，讓理解更順：

| 現在要達成的心理任務 | 建議卡片標題 |
|---|---|
| 先懂定義 | 什麼是臉部平權？ |
| 建立關聯 | 這件事為什麼和我有關？ |
| 打破誤解 | 有些你以為沒惡意的反應，為什麼會傷人？ |
| 看到普遍性 | 這件事在台灣常見嗎？ |
| 看見現實 | 顏損者日常真的會遇到什麼？ |
| 學會互動 | 第一次接觸時，我可以怎麼做？ |
| 轉成行動 | 在學校、職場、社群裡我能做什麼？ |
| 再往下走 | 如果你想更深入，從這裡開始 |

這種排法的關鍵是：每張卡片都在解決一個「下一步問題」，不是只在分類內容。

## 手機 UI/UX 建議

### 導覽列太搶首屏注意力

上方導覽列的存在感很強，尤其黃色按鈕與深色底反差很高，會先搶走一部分焦點。 這對功能導向網站可以接受，但對倡議頁來說，Hero 主張應該是最先被記住的。[[1]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1ad2fc99-b7e3-417b-a52b-7b3ac01d950c/1000009371.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=k68m0DNbrLYcv65VaPLQw9fvaW8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/33eb03e7-0c41-443e-ac40-fa359279b7fb/1000009363.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=rxVLhC0BCqHAxEG2klpspFY%2Ba4M%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E0 ### 卡片陰影、描邊與內文對比可再精簡

現在卡片很多都用了深色底、淡描邊、亮色標題、灰色內文。 問題不是醜，而是當整頁很多區塊都長得有點像時，閱讀節奏會變得平。[[4]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/dc5be7fe-b7cf-4cf2-a96c-5ac62770bcd3/1000009367.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=ztJv6cM3F%2FrsDjq4ShK1p1YNjUQ%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[11]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1710bf4d-f280-472e-8963-3ff266335aa5/1000009347.jpg)[[12]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/190922bb-f12f-4ef4-998a-cd1d29266bf2/1000009349.jpg)[[3]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/a ### 橫滑卡片不適合承載太重要資訊

「真實的聲音」區塊有價值，但如果這些案例是很重要的說服材料，放在橫向滑動裡會降低實際被看完的機率。 手機用戶不是不會滑，而是很多人看見可滑區塊只會滑 1 次就結束。[[13]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg)[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)

## 我會怎麼改版

如果我是你這頁的設計／前端顧問，我會先做這個優先順序：

- 第一優先：重寫首屏與 Hero 下方的「一分鐘理解區」。[[10]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/1c19013f-21e6-4fdf-bcdd-9419e6bccac2/1000009343.jpg)
- 第二優先：把「三件事」與「八張卡片」整併成一條更明確的新手主線。[[7]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2add793a-595c-4ee3-934f-a1a6fc3e2b72/1000009359.jpg)[[8]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/617d54a0-7db1-4e85-97c5-491cdc39379e/1000009355.jpg)
- 第三優先：把真實案例改成更容易讀完的呈現，別太依賴橫滑。[[9]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/2f008b92-59ef-4210-947d-42e244ac81d1/1000009365.jpg?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQLOFVNNR&Signature=LY7x1qN3mJGloZYEfjU7b9KYMnY%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEN%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCIGV6jtWacUv1Jqa%2F%2BBK3U5LebYeFteQTYTtp%2F6ycy5csAiBHP7uOQfm5U7E02Awk2%2FEjvvabptgDplGvm9mz82J6aSr8BAin%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIMuHMLydwJKMyEtqRXKtAE%2BvAm6ePE16VsBXL6lUv%2BJsetfDquCghKxWjVH7tC0L0tA2LA%2B6dEuOz2fbqg8djVQDwM%2BqoF4YmnBM5oLEd2UMkvBlvyggb2W%2FJf2H6GZJ4W3%2FkG3pCRdyTQq%2FoZjMI4WqerhW7MBaalQz8gt%2F38D%2FIhFEN9FEde%2FBXobQpCfyuJQ1gbdUotWJFW8Gzd7bMUUrk9JqRpnHCBoSeMGmT2kPvJgTWoo6oPaAYrPTBDi7j78fB5lccRSLQd5TVKTjST%2BAjoMWMqSN1CtQRi%2FUOuWYVLscIMN6vQJsDZc%2FfWYngaI2ZP0BVpSO6GXBBxwuEk4eHDkNwdBtR4BTYdBcwpgUNfkzuNtGa0QWEVl1ngf4rW3513oUQKfQnZ85sHXBEt2%2FLTUEsJqAPnAqgnt8c%2FgiFQY7juhgQM2eyXOoxJwQnactIACIVV6htYMtPQnqtKZ2Bm0%2By6hWxlDIJ6LYOhxSnWxO1dcveS1jVKXCBOzAd3AqF437mtNQVf6f0t%2B%2BTJ1WyuAQFYZHh7jHqWrRAE2V1DbW3TqqfGuScFUoMAZYpeUzceEVG6%2B7JGa%2Bj0Wv0z19S2F8lOQJqp4cFbiu4BnYh93JUKjZNDuoGdJTJdc3XnN2OCahBgKXIJxLABiiKE8EcHJNm9MDUcWx1%2FdprmVXPsC%2FzQI60DX0MNdvgJRfEGc40KwMOIjANVW1guwGVBaE3mdp14z97BwTOLXW%2BTWlJdjglI9j%2Fvgcvj%2FNCBuKMhiWVQVW6PUmQ2i5EtmfcSsOFsDi33tcbOy%2FuBXARgjTCu2bbPBjqZAdRMT%2BGYeuxVdOiDbaqmNxodD6nHtbcA%2FHe2Mvct2Nwo4%2BvRivUean7JxycG8ExiTTxTrxJDjtarRYgDkhOHuYU%2FbXKTQsXKzI7fHGs4qdA0Lam5BjbuEwUZmHwzNZ1nW8S%2FE64%2FjHIE%2B7iAcAkrpMoKDJHLuwNCCO7uSoG6EVOB3th5vK6heVf2%2Fj1j9ibUXEWhR6NZUFIdpw%3D%3D&Expires=1777186087)[[13]](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/images/122048128/4f2b396e-9d8e-4c4b-9ee7-6750f7b650d2/1000009345.jpg)

## 你下一步最值得做的事
